```diff
+  key: {
+    A: {
+      item: "pamhc2foodextended:lemondrizzlecakeitem"
+    }
+    B: {
```

```diff
+  neoforge:conditions: [
+    {
+      type: "neoforge:mod_loaded"
+      modid: "immersiveengineering"
+    }
+  ]
+  type: "mekmm:stamper"
+  main_input: {
+    count: 1
+    tag: "c:ingots/constantan"
+  }
+  mold: {
+    count: 1
+    item: "immersiveengineering:mold_plate"
+  }
+  output: {
+    count: 1
+    id: "alltheores:constantan_plate"
+  }
+}

```


</details>

```diff
       }
```

```diff
     amount: 710
```
